 hamen ummid he ki ab, pathankot main jo hua or haal main uri main hua, uski punrariti nahin hogi
 We feel that the government should ensure the safety of its people from cross-border terrorism
 yechuri ne kaha ki hamen ummid he ki ab aage takaraav main or vruddhi nahin hogi
 He urged the Center to continue diplomatic and political steps to end cross-border terrorism and reduce tensions
 yah puche jane par ki sipiem pakistan ke saath kyon baatcheet ke paksh main he, jabaki vigat main aise prayaas naakaam rahe hai, yechuri ne kaha ki kuch media samooh hai jo ham par (sipiem) rajdroh kaa aarope thopanaa chaahate hai
 He questioned what is in the interest of the country? He said that indo-pak talks are on the declared agenda of this government
 unhone daawa kiya ki desh kii videsh niti main 'america kii ore jhukaav' ise america virdohi aatankwaadi samoohon kaa nishaanaa bana rahaa he

 janata pradhanmantri narendra modi ko isi vajah se pasand karti he

 bhale hi notebandi se log daawa kar rahe hai ki logon kaa rojgaar chhina he, kuch sector kaa kahana he ki unhen ghaataa hua he, lekin isse bhrashtachar par lagaam laga he
 Modi 2 made of demonetisation

 ' An alleged case of beating a Dalit groom on a mare in Rajasthan's Udaipur district has come to light
 ek aaropee ko hiraasat main liya gaya
 Based on a complaint lodged by a Dalit groom at Udaipur's Ghassa police, police have registered a case under the SC / ST Act late last night against four accused and one accused has been detained, while others are being searched 
 police ne bataaya ki udaipur ke jhaalo kaa dhana gaanv main guuruuvaar raat dalit duulhaa kailash meghavaal (25) kii baraat ja rahi thi, usee dauraan paanch chah logon ne baratiyon ke saath laathiyon, dhardaar hathiyaaron or bear kii botalon se hamalaa kar diya or duulhe meghavaal ko ghodi se utaar kar pitayee kii gai
 The comments police ke anusaar darj shikaayat main bataaya gaya ki rajput bahulya kshetra main anusuchit jati ke logon ko ghodi par savaar nahin hone diya jaataa he
 The head and body of the groom have been hurt and solder
 ghasa thanadhikari ramesh kavia ne bataaya ki darj shikaayat ke aadhaar par aaropee kaalu singh, nepal singh, rajendra singh or kishan singh ke khilaaf essi / asti adhinium ke tahat maamla darj kar jaanch shuru kar di gai he
 Additional police force has been deployed in the area as a precautionary measure
 udaipur ke ghasa thane main dalit duulhe kii ore se darj shikaayat ke aadhaar par police ne chaar aropiyon ke khilaaf kal der raat essi / asti adhinium ke tahat maamla darj kar ek aaropee ko hiraasat main liya gaya he, jabaki anya kii talash kii ja rahi he
 Police said that Dalit groom Kailash Meghwal (25) was going to a wedding procession in Jhana's Dhana village of Udaipur on Thursday night, while five people attacked him with sticks, sharpened weapons and beer bottles, and the groom Meghwal
 Was beaten up and beaten by a mare
 tippaniyan According to the complaint lodged by the police, it was told that scheduled caste people are not allowed to ride on mares in Rajput dominated areas
 duulhe ke sir or sharir par chot lagi he or taanken aae he
 Grass station officer Ramesh Kavia said that on the basis of the complaint lodged, investigation has been initiated against the accused Kalu Singh, Nepal Singh, Rajendra Singh and Kishan Singh under the SC / ST Act
 kshetra main aihtiyaat ke taur par atirikt police bal tainaat kiya gaya he
